 Our clothes play an important role in making us attractive and beautiful
 hamaare kapade or hamaara fishan statement kaaphi had tak hamaare impressant ko bana bhi saktaa he or bigaad bhi saktaa he
 Apart from this, our clothes also make us look fat or thin
 agar aapako bhi lagata he ki aapkaa motopa aapaki luk ko kharaab kar rahaa he, to aap apane kapade pahanane ke andaaj main kuch badlaav kar ke slim or atractive dikh sakati hai
 Let's know how
 
 
 1
 Sitting and walking in the right posture makes you look more slim and confident
 good posture kaa matlab he ki aapke kaan, kandhe or chin jamine ke bilkul paralel hone chahie
 Keep your waist perfectly straight and your feet parallel to the ground
 2
 Wear only clothes with perfect fitting
 dhyaan rakhen ki aapane jo kapade pahane hai, wo naa zyada deele hone chahie or naa zyada tite hone chahie
 Wearing clothes of perfect fitting not only gives support to your body, you also look slim
 3
 Try wearing dark colored clothes
 aap chahen to blike, grey, purple, brown rang ke kapade chun sakati hai

 atractive or slim luk paane ke liye jaruri he ki aap sahi sies ke kapade pahanen

 After facing all-round criticism on this issue, the authorities have requested the parents of the student to send her to school daily from home
